style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:125%">Gossamer Bio Announces Fourth Quarter and Full-Year 2021 Financial style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">- GB004 topline results for the Phase 2 SHIFT-UC study in mild-to-moderate UC expected in the second quarter of 2022 -</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">- Seralutinib (GB002) topline results for the Phase 2 TORREY study in PAH expected in the second half of 2022, subject to developments in the ongoing COVID-19 pandemic -</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:center"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">- Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities totaled $325 million at year-end 2021 -</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">SAN DIEGO &#8212; (BUSINESS WIRE) &#8212; March&#160;3, 2022 &#8212; Gossamer Bio, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; GOSS), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on discovering, acquiring, developing and commercializing therapeutics in the disease areas of immunology, inflammation and oncology, today announced its financial results for the fourth quarter and year ended December 31, 2021 and provided a business update.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;After a considerable amount of planning and effort, the Gossamer team is excited to enter 2022 with two ongoing Phase 2 trials expected to readout this year,&#8221; said Faheem Hasnain, Co-Founder, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of Gossamer Bio.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;In the near term, we are eager to review GB004 Phase 2 SHIFT-UC 12-week topline data in patients with mild-to-moderate ulcerative colitis in the second quarter. We believe that, in contrast to other IBD therapies, GB004 has the potential to restore the epithelial barrier without systemic immune suppression. If this thesis bears out, GB004 could address the large swath of ulcerative colitis patients who are reticent to progress to systemic immunomodulatory or biologic agents, despite their disease being uncontrolled by 5-ASA therapy.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Clinical-Stage Product Candidate Updates</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">GB004&#58; Oral HIF-1&#945; Stabilizer for Inflammatory Bowel Disease (IBD)</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Primary endpoint week 12 topline data from the Phase 2 SHIFT-UC study in patients with mild-to-moderate ulcerative colitis (UC) are expected in the second quarter of 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Treat through week 36 topline data from the Phase 2 SHIFT-UC study in patients with mild-to-moderate UC are expected in the fourth quarter of 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Seralutinib (GB002)&#58; Inhaled PDGFR, CSF1R and c-KIT Inhibitor for Pulmonary Arterial Hypertension (PAH)</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Enrollment ongoing in the TORREY Study, a Phase 2 clinical trial in patients with PAH whose disease has progressed despite standard-of-care therapy. The primary endpoint is change in pulmonary vascular resistance from baseline at week 24. Topline data from the TORREY study are expected in the second half of 2022, subject to developments in the ongoing COVID-19 pandemic.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">GB5121&#58; Oral, CNS-Penetrant BTK Inhibitor for Primary CNS Lymphoma (PCNSL)</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.8pt">An investigational new drug application (IND) application for GB5121 is now active, following a fourth quarter filing with the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA).</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.8pt">Gossamer expects to initiate a global Phase 1b&#47;2 clinical trial of GB5121 in PCNSL patients in the first half of 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Financial Results for Quarter and Full Year Ended December 31, 2021</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Cash, Cash Equivalents and Marketable Securities</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities as of December 31, 2021, were $325.2 million. As a result, we currently expect cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities, and access to our debt facility will be sufficient to fund operating and capital expenditures into the second half of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.13pt">Research and Development (R&#38;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; For the quarter ended December 31, 2021, R&#38;D expenses were $40.9 million compared to R&#38;D expenses of $38.9 million for the same period in 2020. R&#38;D expenses for the full year ended December 31, 2021, were $170.3 million compared to $160.9 million for the full year ended December 31, 2020.</font><font style="color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> The increase was primarily attributable to an increase of clinical trial and preclinical study costs associated with seralutinib, GB004, GB5121, and preclinical programs. This increase was partially offset by decreases in clinical trial and preclinical study costs related to GB001 and GB1275. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%;padding-left:13.13pt">In-Process Research and Development (IPR&#38;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#58; There were no significant IPR&#38;D expenses for the quarter and year ended December 31, 2021. For the quarter ended December 31, 2020, IPR&#38;D expenses were $5.3 million. IPR&#38;D expenses for the full year ended December 31, 2020, were $23.4 million.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">General and Administrative (G&#38;A) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; For the quarter ended December 31, 2021, G&#38;A expenses were $10.7 million compared to $15.9 million for the same period in 2020. G&#38;A expenses for the full year ended December 31, 2021, were $45.8 million compared to $49.7 million for the full year ended December 31, 2020.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Net Loss</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#58; Net loss for the three months ended December 31, 2021, was $56.3 million, or $0.74 per share, compared to a net loss of $64.6 million, or $1.05 per share, for the same period in 2020. Net loss for the full year ended December 31, 2021, was $234.0 million, or $3.13 per share compared to a net loss of $243.4 million, or $3.55 per share, for the full year ended December 31, 2020.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Conference Call and Webcast</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gossamer&#8217;s management team will host a conference call and live audio webcast at 4&#58;30 p.m. ET today,  Thursday, March&#160;3, to discuss its fourth quarter and full year 2021 financial results and provide a corporate update.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The live audio webcast may be accessed through the &#8220;Events &#47; Presentations&#8221; page in the &#8220;Investors&#8221; section of the Company's website at </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0000ff;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">www.gossamerbio.com</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0a0a0a;font-family:'Cambria',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">.
